## Get $10,000 in Rebates - Dual Fuel Heat Pump + Gas Furnace

![Our service expert walking from a customer's house to our blue and green work truck. The background has a slight blur or bokeh for ambiance.](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

By combining the power of a gas furnace with the efficiency of a heat pump, dual fuel systems provide optimal warmth while saving on energy costs.

Book your FREE estimate today to see how this smart, cost-effective solution can work for your home. Call now to schedule!

[CALL (604) 245-2550](tel:604-245-2550)

![Our HVAC service expert poses with a High mark shirt and freshly installed heat pump in the background. High Mark's "What's an Dual Fuel System static image that is featured in our Facebook ad.](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

Eligibility:

- Lived in your home for at least 12 months
- Haven‚Äôt gotten a furnace rebate for at least 10 years.
- Must be replacing an existing gas furnace that is at least 10 years old.
- Must be a new central ducted air source heat pump that is connected to a compatible high-efficiency gas furnace.
- Warranty replacements and insurance claims are not eligible for this rebate.
- Must be installed by a Technical Safety BC licensed gas contractor.

![Our HVAC service expert poses with a High mark shirt and freshly installed heat pump in the background. High Mark's "What's an Dual Fuel System static image that is featured in our Facebook ad.](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

## Benefits of Dual Fuel Heat Pump Systems

During your initial consultation, our HVAC specialist will assess your home‚Äôs unique heating and cooling needs to recommend the optimal dual fuel heat pump system.

You‚Äôll receive a tailored set of options and clear, upfront pricing to make a confident, informed choice. Once you‚Äôre ready, we can begin as soon as the next day‚Äîand have your home warmed up the same day!

Discover the benefits of switching to a dual fuel system:

- **Energy Efficiency:** Saves on energy costs by using the heat pump for moderate temperatures and the furnace for extreme cold.
- **Enhanced Comfort:** Provides consistent warmth by automatically switching to the best heating option based on the weather.
- **Lower Utility Bills:** Reduces gas usage during milder weather, helping you save money on monthly heating costs.
- **Eco-Friendly:** Reduces carbon footprint by optimizing energy use, especially during moderate temperatures.
- **Versatile Performance:** Ideal for varying climates, ensuring efficient heating in winter and cooling in summer.
- **Additional $150 rebate for Connected Smart Thermostat:** We'll install a thermostat that is eligible for this specific rebate.

# **REBATES ‚Äì IN BRITISH COLUMBIA**

Various rebates are available on new HVAC installations in British Columbia. Here is a list of available rebates, separated by appliance.¬† Please note, they are subject to change depending on various factors.

_Information valid as of December 2, 2024_

## BC Hydro Bonus Rebates

![Blue Check](<Base64-Image-Removed>)¬† ¬† ¬† Rebates for Home Renovations ‚Äì Receive up to $10,000 back in rebates with [BC Hydro](https://www.bchydro.com/powersmart/residential/rebates-programs/home-renovation.html)

![Blue Check](<Base64-Image-Removed>)¬† ¬† ¬† With two or more energy-efficient upgrades ‚Äì Get $300 to $2000 back in rebates with [BC Hydro](https://www.bchydro.com/powersmart/residential/rebates-programs/home-renovation/bonus-rebates.html)

## Furnace Rebates

#### Available Province Wide

![Blue Check](<Base64-Image-Removed>)¬† ¬† ¬† Eligible Smart Thermostats ‚Äì¬† $25 OFF with a [FortisBC](https://www.fortisbc.com/rebates-and-energy-savings/rebates-and-offers?l=)rebate for income-qualified households

![Blue Check](<Base64-Image-Removed>)¬† ¬† ¬† Annual Furnace Servicing ‚Äì Rebate of up to $150 with a [FortisBC](https://www.fortisbc.com/rebates/home/appliance-maintenance-program)rebate¬† ‚Äì _Valid until June 30, 2025_.

[**Urgent Update: Dual Fuel Heating System Rebates**](https://www.fortisbc.com/rebates/detail/dual-fuel-heating-system-rebate-income-qualified)

**Secure a $10,000 Rebate Before It Drops to $5,000!**

**Installations Completed by April 30, 2025:**

- Ensure your invoice and mobile app commissioning sheet are both dated no later than April 30, 2025.


**Installations Completed Between May 1 and May 31, 2025:**

- Rebate amount is $5,000.
- Obtain a quote and provide a paid deposit by April 30, 2025.
- Ensure both your invoice and commissioning sheet are dated no later than May 31, 2025.

**All Applicants:**

- Rebate applications must be submitted within six months of the installation date.
- Must be a year-round primary residence in British Columbia with a residential utility account.
- Applies to single-family homes, duplexes, or townhomes with separate meters.
- Additional rebates may be available if switching from oil, propane, or natural gas to a dual-fuel system.
- Your installation must be completed by a licensed contractor.

## Why Choose a Dual Fuel System for Your Home?

At High Mark Plumbing & Heating, we understand the importance of optimizing your home‚Äôs comfort and efficiency.

A dual fuel system combines a high-efficiency heat pump with a reliable furnace, intelligently switching between electric and gas heating based on outdoor temperatures and energy costs‚Äîoffering a versatile solution tailored to our diverse climate.

Whether you prefer Canadian-crafted options or other high-quality systems, we provide personalized options and expert installation to ensure your home benefits from the best fit for your needs.

- **Year-Round Comfort:** The heat pump handles milder weather, while the furnace kicks in during colder days, ensuring consistent warmth.
- **Energy Savings:** Automatically switches to the most cost-effective fuel source, potentially lowering your heating costs compared to a single-system setup.
- **Eco-Friendly Choice:** Reduces reliance on fossil fuels by optimizing heat pump use, aligning with sustainable living goals.
- **Durable & Reliable:** Canadian-made design built to withstand local conditions, backed by Highmark Plumbing‚Äôs expert installation and support.
- **Up to $14,000 Back in Rebates:** you may qualify for rebates to offset costs through the CleanBC Better Homes and Home Renovation Rebate Program.
- **Smart Thermostat:** Additional rebates are available for those who opt to install an eligible smart thermostat.

# Get up to $150 back with the Fortis BC Maintenance Rebate

Get up to $150 back with the Fortis BC Maintenance Rebate! Keep your furnace, boiler, or tankless water heater running efficiently and your home cozy. Book your annual service today!

## Get up to $150 back with the Fortis BC Maintenance Rebate

![Our service expert walking from a customer's house to our blue and green work truck. The background has a slight blur or bokeh for ambiance.](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

Get up to $150 back with the Fortis BC Maintenance Rebate! Keep your furnace, boiler, or tankless water heater running efficiently and your home cozy. Book your annual service today!

Don‚Äôt miss this chance to save money and enjoy peace of mind‚Äîbook your annual service today!

[CALL (604) 330-1780](tel:604-330-1780)

![Get up to $150 back in rebate with Fortis BC! This image showcases an image of an iPhone with the first look at the Fortis web page.](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

Eligibility:

- Must have your appliance serviced by a licensed gas contractor.
- Service must be completed between June 1, 2024 to June 30, 2025
- Furnace or Boiler service: $50 rebate
- Tankless water heater service: $50 rebate
- Maximum rebate available: up to $150 back
- Hot water tanks (storage tanks) are not eligible for this rebate.
- Homeowners are responsible of checking eligibility and applying for this rebate.

Learn more [about the rebate](https://www.fortisbc.com/rebates/detail/appliance-maintenance-program)!

![Get up to $150 back in rebate with Fortis BC! This image showcases an image of an iPhone with the first look at the Fortis web page.](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

## Why is Annual Maintenance Essential?

Don‚Äôt let the holiday season catch you off guard with a sudden breakdown. Scheduling annual maintenance ensures your heating system operates efficiently, safely, and reliably when you need it most. Stay ahead of costly surprises and enjoy consistent warmth and hot water all winter long.

- **Avoid Expensive Emergencies:** Our experts will fix minor issues before they turn into costly repairs.
- **Lower Energy Bills:** Keep your system running at peak efficiency and save on monthly heating costs.
- **Extend the Lifespan of Your System:** Protect your investment and avoid early replacements
- **Ensure Safety:** Catch potential hazards like carbon monoxide leaks early.
- **Uninterrupted Comfort:** Prevent breakdowns during freezing weather when reliability is critical
- **Stay Warranty-Compliant:** Many warranties require routine maintenance to remain valid.

## 24/7 Emergency Plumbing Services

Finding yourself in need of a plumbing disaster? An unexpected plumbing emergency can arise at any time. High Mark provides expert emergency plumbing services at all hours including evenings, weekends, and holidays. We‚Äôre here for you to restore your peace of mind.

When you are facing a plumbing emergency, in Port Coquitlam or any of the Tri-Cities, there is only one name to contact. Once we are notified, we send our service expert to you as soon as possible to rescue you from your plumbing disasters.

At [High Mark](https://highmarkplumbing.com/), we are committed to providing the best in 24/7 emergency plumbing services. If you find yourself in a plumbing crisis, don‚Äôt wait. Call us right away and let‚Äôs get your emergency plumbing issues resolved without further stress.

Although we were unable to reproduce the leak, he did show pictures of where water stains had occurred and these were all above the drain. ## Emergency Plumbing Services in Tri-Cities (Port Coquitlam, Coquitlam, Port Moody) We Provide

When you have a severe clog or water damage in your Port Coquitlam, Coquitlam or Port Moody home, it‚Äôs often due to a few common reasons. Because plumbing emergencies can happen at any time, 24/7 emergency plumbing services are a must.

### Burst Pipes

[Burst pipes](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/burst-pipe-repair/) are a homeowner‚Äôs worst nightmare. When it rains heavily or the snow melts, burst pipes can suddenly occur. This is quite a popular reason for pipes bursting in Port Coquitlam. This is an urgent matter, requiring professional [plumbing services](https://highmarkplumbing.com/cambie-plumbing/). Contact our emergency plumbing service option right way.

### Severely Clogged Drains

Have you ever noticed sewage coming up from your drains or toilets? [Clogged drains](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/clogged-drains/) aren‚Äôt just bad for your health; they can also cause severe damage to your home. We understand how messy and dire [clogged sewer lines](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/sewer-services/) can be. Our Port Coquitlam and Tri-Cities plumbing service experts are ready to address your plumbing emergency, fix the problem and restore smooth flowing drains in your home.

### Overflowing Toilet

Having your plumbing checked at least once a year helps prevent major water damage and other costly repairs. With High Mark‚Äôs [annual inspection](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/plumbing/), our service experts thoroughly examine your systems including water pressure, running toilets, leaks, and loose components. We‚Äôll provide you with a detailed report and suggest [any fixes or replacements](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/toilet-services/) to keep your plumbing systems functioning at their best. Trust us to help keep your home dry and in great condition.

### Leaky Pipes and Fixtures

Have you ever laid awake at night, disturbed by the sound of dripping within your walls or ceiling? Ensure your leaky pipes don‚Äôt compromise your sleep. Our plumbing service experts are here to [resolve your leaky pipe problems](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/leak-repair/) once and for all! If you have a leak or a broken faucet, let us fix it and stop that dripping for good.

### Water Heater Not Working

No matter the day, cold showers are always an unwelcome surprise. You might not think about your hot water tank much because it doesn‚Äôt need checks every year, but when it breaks, it‚Äôs urgent and in need of an emergency plumbing service. Whether your water heater is or a traditional tank, our service experts can [replace it fast](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/water-heater-installation/). If you don‚Äôt have hot water, call High Mark immediately. Say goodbye to cold showers!

### Broken Watermain or Drain Tile

Are you suspecting a [burst watermain](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/water-line-repair/) or drain tile? In Port Coquitlam and surrounding cities, where heavy rain is a common occurrence, it‚Äôs essential to have your [drain tile](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/drain-tile-services/) ready to take on the excess water. When you notice water pooling, low water pressure, or the city sends a notice, we‚Äôre here to fix your [broken underground pipes](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/burst-pipe-repair/), minimizing damage and stress. Call us anytime, day or night, for immediate assistance.

### Sump Pump Failure

Sump pumps are often found in your basement or outside your home. They help prevent devastating floods indoors. When your [sump pump stops working](https://highmarkplumbing.com/services/sump-pump/), it can lead to significant water damage. It‚Äôs important to tackle the repair right away to ensure your Port Coquitlam (or anywhere in the Tri-Cities) home remains dry and prevent further damage.

## Warning Signs that Indicate a Plumbing Emergency

Plumbing problems can show early, silent signs before turning into an emergency. Look out for these signs to catch the problem before they get worse:

- **Unpleasant Odours:** Foul odours from your drains typically happen from clogs and sewer line problems.
- **Spike in Water Meter or Bills:** Regularly check your water bills and take action when a notice from the city arrives I the mail. This can help uncover hidden problems in your plumbing systems.
- **Gurgling and Bubbling Sounds:** This often signals sewer line problems which tends to be a severe clog deeper down the line.
- **Specific Lush Areas in Your Landscaping:** Lush spots indicate possible leak in your watermain, sewer line, or drain tile giving extra hydration and fertilizer to the soil.
- **Mold, Mildew, and Pest Problems:** When there‚Äôs moisture and humidity lingering in the walls and crawlspaces, you may find unwelcome pests in your home, often indicating a leak or burst pipe.

## What is a Heating Emergency?

When temperatures drop, prompt action is essential to keep you and your heating system safe. We‚Äôre here 24/7 to address any of the following problems at all hours:

- **System Not Heating Your Home:** When you have no heat, quick professional help is essential to stay safe and warm. Call us right away to make sure your home is safe, and your system runs smoothly again.
- **Carbon Monoxide Warning:** This gas is a health hazard and can cause fatalities. Contact us immediately so we can ensure a safe home for you to return to.
- **Odd Noises or Smells:** Strange sounds or smells suggest serious internal issues that can worsen without fast, expert help.
- **Cycling System:** If your system keeps turning on and off, not only does it waste energy but also indicates a problem in your system that needs urgent attention.
- **Leaks:** Water leaking from your heating system can damage your home and suggest a malfunction that requires prompt fixing.
- **Electrical Problems:** When your heating is on and your lights flicker or breakers trip, your heating system may have electrical issues that need immediate professional care.

## Call High Mark for Fast, 24/7 Emergency Heating Service

Caught in the cold with a heating breakdown? Don‚Äôt let a chilly home disrupt your comfort. When temperatures drop, we‚Äôre here to turn the heat up. With our 24-hour emergency heating service in Greater Vancouver, prompt, professional help is just a call away. Stay warm, safe, and secure, regardless of the weather. Contact us now and let us bring the heat back to your home!

## Financing Options

Do you need some plumbing, heating or electrical work but are short on cash?

No matter if it is an emergency repair or a new installation, High Mark is more than happy to offer a financing solution through Finance It.

### Benefits

- Stress-free approval process
- Timeframe of term is adjustable - From 12 months to 15 years
- Interest rates vary depending on loan amount
- Interest rates never go over 10.99%
- Pay off balance with no penalty
- Canadian Company
- No Hidden Fees
